\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+export\+\_\+keys\+\_\+t}{mbedtls\_ssl\_export\_keys\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+export\+\_\+keys\+\_\+t(void $\ast$p\+\_\+expkey, const unsigned char $\ast$ms, const unsigned char $\ast$kb, size\+\_\+t maclen, size\+\_\+t keylen, size\+\_\+t ivlen)}



Callback type\+: Export key block and master secret. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is required for certain uses of T\+LS, e.\+g. E\+A\+P-\/\+T\+LS (R\+FC 5216) and Thread. The key pointers are ephemeral and therefore must not be stored. The master secret and keys should not be used directly except as an input to a key derivation function.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+\_\+expkey} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_context}{Context}} for the callback \\
\hline
{\em ms} & Pointer to master secret (fixed length\+: 48 bytes) \\
\hline
{\em kb} & Pointer to key block, see R\+FC 5246 section 6.\+3 (variable length\+: 2 $\ast$ maclen + 2 $\ast$ keylen + 2 $\ast$ ivlen). \\
\hline
{\em maclen} & M\+AC length \\
\hline
{\em keylen} & Key length \\
\hline
{\em ivlen} & IV length\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or a specific M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+X\+XX code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em buf} & Buffer to write the received data to \\
\hline
{\em len} & Length of the receive buffer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The callback must return the number of bytes received, or a non-\/zero error code. If performing non-\/blocking I/O, {\ttfamily M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+AD} must be returned when the operation would block.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\end{DoxyNote}

Callback type\+: receive data from the network, with timeout. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
That callback must block until data is received, or the timeout delay expires, or the operation is interrupted by a signal.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer\+\_\+t@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer\+\_\+t}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer\+\_\+t}{mbedtls\_ssl\_set\_timer\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer\+\_\+t(void $\ast$ctx, uint32\+\_\+t int\+\_\+ms, uint32\+\_\+t fin\+\_\+ms)}



Callback type\+: set a pair of timers/delays to watch. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_context}{Context}} pointer \\
\hline
{\em int\+\_\+ms} & Intermediate delay in milliseconds \\
\hline
{\em fin\+\_\+ms} & Final delay in milliseconds 0 cancels the current timer.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This callback must at least store the necessary information for the associated {\ttfamily mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+timer\+\_\+t} callback to return correct information.

If using a event-\/driven style of programming, an event must be generated when the final delay is passed. The event must cause a call to {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake()}}} with the proper S\+SL context to be scheduled. Care must be taken to ensure that at most one such call happens at a time.

Only one timer at a time must be running. Calling this function while a timer is running must cancel it. Cancelled timers must not generate any event. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+ticket\+\_\+parse\+\_\+t}{mbedtls\_ssl\_ticket\_parse\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+ticket\+\_\+parse\+\_\+t(void $\ast$p\+\_\+ticket, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__session}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$session, unsigned char $\ast$buf, size\+\_\+t len)}



Callback type\+: parse and load session ticket. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This describes what a callback implementation should do. This callback should parse a session ticket as generated by the corresponding mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+ticket\+\_\+write\+\_\+t function, and, if the ticket is authentic and valid, load the session.

The implementation is allowed to modify the first len bytes of the input buffer, eg to use it as a temporary area for the decrypted ticket contents.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+\_\+ticket} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_context}{Context}} for the callback \\
\hline
{\em session} & S\+SL session to be loaded \\
\hline
{\em buf} & Start of the buffer containing the ticket \\
\hline
{\em len} & Length of the ticket.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+M\+AC if not authentic, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+S\+E\+S\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+T\+I\+C\+K\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+I\+R\+ED if expired, or any other non-\/zero code for other failures. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Callback type\+: generate and write session ticket. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This describes what a callback implementation should do. This callback should generate an encrypted and authenticated ticket for the session and write it to the output buffer. Here, ticket means the opaque ticket part of the New\+Session\+Ticket structure of R\+FC 5077.

Disable or enable support for R\+C4 (Default\+: M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+R\+C4\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED) 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Use of R\+C4 in D\+T\+L\+S/\+T\+LS has been prohibited by R\+FC 7465 for security reasons. Use at your own risk.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function is deprecated and will likely be removed in a future version of the library. R\+C4 is disabled by default at compile time and needs to be actively enabled for use with legacy systems.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+authmode@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+authmode}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+authmode()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_authmode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+authmode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int}]{authmode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the certificate verification mode Default\+: N\+O\+NE on server, R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED on client. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em authmode} & can be\+:\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE\+: peer certificate is not checked (default on server) (insecure on client)

M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL\+: peer certificate is checked, however the handshake continues even if verification failed; \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a516064f1468d459159ef7cd6c496a026}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+verify\+\_\+result()}} can be called after the handshake is complete.

M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED\+: peer {\itshape must} present a valid certificate, handshake is aborted if verification failed. (default on client)

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
On client, M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED is the recommended mode. With M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+AL, the user needs to call \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a516064f1468d459159ef7cd6c496a026}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+verify\+\_\+result()}} at the right time(s), which may not be obvious, while R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED always perform the verification as soon as possible. For example, R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED was protecting against the \char`\"{}triple handshake\char`\"{} attack even before it was found. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a85c3bb6b682ba361d13de1c0a1eb69fb}\label{ssl_8h_a85c3bb6b682ba361d13de1c0a1eb69fb}}

Set the X.\+509 security profile used for verification. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The restrictions are enforced for all certificates in the chain. However, signatures in the handshake are not covered by this setting but by {\bfseries \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a73725fed867e0fd29396c7c6565a76e6}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sig\+\_\+hashes()}}}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em profile} & Profile to use \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_ac8e4df37cadda8f743ed45501a51fec1}\label{ssl_8h_ac8e4df37cadda8f743ed45501a51fec1}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_ciphersuites()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{const int $\ast$}]{ciphersuites }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the list of allowed ciphersuites and the preference order. First in the list has the highest preference. (Overrides all version-\/specific lists) 

The ciphersuites array is not copied, and must remain valid for the lifetime of the ssl\+\_\+config.

Note\+: The server uses its own preferences over the preference of the client unless M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+S\+R\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+P\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+F\+E\+R\+E\+N\+CE is defined!

{\em ciphersuites} & 0-\/terminated list of allowed ciphersuites \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites\+\_\+for\+\_\+version (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{const int $\ast$}]{ciphersuites,  }\item[{int}]{major,  }\item[{int}]{minor }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The ciphersuites array is not copied, and must remain valid for the lifetime of the ssl\+\_\+config.

\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_ae1d705b8fc48224262ab92eb5aa4598c}\label{ssl_8h_ae1d705b8fc48224262ab92eb5aa4598c}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+curves@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+curves}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+curves@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+curves}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+curves()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_curves()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+curves (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{ecp_8h_af79e530ea8f8416480f805baa20b1a2d}{mbedtls\+\_\+ecp\+\_\+group\+\_\+id}} $\ast$}]{curves }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the allowed curves in order of preference. (Default\+: all defined curves.) 

On server\+: this only affects selection of the E\+C\+D\+HE curve; the curves used for E\+C\+DH and E\+C\+D\+SA are determined by the list of available certificates instead.

On client\+: this affects the list of curves offered for any use. The server can override our preference order.

Both sides\+: limits the set of curves accepted for use in E\+C\+D\+HE and in the peer\textquotesingle{}s end-\/entity certificate.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This has no influence on which curves are allowed inside the certificate chains, see {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a76dc3c312ffd51f6d0ca127b322307bb}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+cert\+\_\+profile()}}} for that. For the end-\/entity certificate however, the key will be accepted only if it is allowed both by this list and by the cert profile.

This list should be ordered by decreasing preference (preferred curve first).
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em curves} & Ordered list of allowed curves, terminated by M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+C\+P\+\_\+\+D\+P\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+anti\+\_\+replay@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+anti\+\_\+replay}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+anti\+\_\+replay@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+anti\+\_\+replay}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+anti\+\_\+replay()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_dtls\_anti\_replay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+anti\+\_\+replay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{char}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable or disable anti-\/replay protection for D\+T\+LS. (D\+T\+LS only, no effect on T\+LS.) Default\+: enabled. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em mode} & M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+N\+T\+I\+\_\+\+R\+E\+P\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+ED or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+N\+T\+I\+\_\+\+R\+E\+P\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Disabling this is a security risk unless the application protocol handles duplicated packets in a safe way. You should not disable this without careful consideration. However, if your application already detects duplicated packets and needs information about them to adjust its transmission strategy, then you\textquotesingle{}ll want to disable this. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a9baa37a4b839319d00d8b43c8d266719}\label{ssl_8h_a9baa37a4b839319d00d8b43c8d266719}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+badmac\+\_\+limit@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+badmac\+\_\+limit}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+badmac\+\_\+limit@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+badmac\+\_\+limit}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+badmac\+\_\+limit()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_dtls\_badmac\_limit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+badmac\+\_\+limit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{unsigned}]{limit }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set a limit on the number of records with a bad M\+AC before terminating the connection. (D\+T\+LS only, no effect on T\+LS.) Default\+: 0 (disabled). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em limit} & Limit, or 0 to disable.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the limit is N, then the connection is terminated when the Nth non-\/authentic record is seen.

Records with an invalid header are not counted, only the ones going through the authentication-\/decryption phase.

This is a security trade-\/off related to the fact that it\textquotesingle{}s often relatively easy for an active attacker ot inject U\+DP datagrams. On one hand, setting a low limit here makes it easier for such an attacker to forcibly terminated a connection. On the other hand, a high limit or no limit might make us waste resources checking authentication on many bogus packets. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a5865631bc70b4511c25f558d5221fd65}\label{ssl_8h_a5865631bc70b4511c25f558d5221fd65}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+cookies@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+cookies}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+cookies@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+cookies}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+cookies()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_dtls\_cookies()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+dtls\+\_\+cookies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a536f8b89936f26732150b00639a47ff0}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+cookie\+\_\+write\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{f\+\_\+cookie\+\_\+write,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a9cfda5aee70d6c2c19a8dfb5af900d80}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+cookie\+\_\+check\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{f\+\_\+cookie\+\_\+check,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\+\_\+cookie }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Register callbacks for D\+T\+LS cookies (Server only. D\+T\+LS only.) 

Default\+: dummy callbacks that fail, in order to force you to register working callbacks (and initialize their context).

To disable Hello\+Verify\+Request, register N\+U\+LL callbacks.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Disabling hello verification allows your server to be used for amplification in DoS attacks against other hosts. Only disable if you known this can\textquotesingle{}t happen in your particular environment.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
See comments on {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake()}}} about handling the M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+L\+L\+O\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED that is expected on the first handshake attempt when this is enabled.

This is also necessary to handle client reconnection from the same port as described in R\+FC 6347 section 4.\+2.\+8 (only the variant with cookies is supported currently). See comments on {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read()}}} for details.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\

{\em f\+\_\+cookie\+\_\+write} & Cookie write callback \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+cookie\+\_\+check} & Cookie check callback \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+cookie} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_context}{Context}} for both callbacks \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+extended\+\_\+master\+\_\+secret@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+extended\+\_\+master\+\_\+secret}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+extended\+\_\+master\+\_\+secret@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+extended\+\_\+master\+\_\+secret}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+extended\+\_\+master\+\_\+secret()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_extended\_master\_secret()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+extended\+\_\+master\+\_\+secret (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{char}]{ems }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable or disable Extended Master Secret negotiation. (Default\+: M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+D\+E\+D\+\_\+\+M\+S\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+ED) 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This should always be enabled, it is a security fix to the protocol, and should not cause any interoperability issue (used only if the peer supports it too).
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em ems} & M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+D\+E\+D\+\_\+\+M\+S\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+ED or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+E\+N\+D\+E\+D\+\_\+\+M\+S\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_abb5a878b9aabe137572a8c73a840c480}\label{ssl_8h_abb5a878b9aabe137572a8c73a840c480}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+fallback@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+fallback}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+fallback@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+fallback}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+fallback()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_fallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+fallback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{char}]{fallback }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the fallback flag (client-\/side only). (Default\+: M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK). 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Set to M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK when preparing a fallback connection, that is a connection with max\+\_\+version set to a lower value than the value you\textquotesingle{}re willing to use. Such fallback connections are not recommended but are sometimes necessary to interoperate with buggy (version-\/intolerant) servers.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
You should N\+OT set this to M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK for non-\/fallback connections! This would appear to work for a while, then cause failures when the server is upgraded to support a newer T\+LS version.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em fallback} & M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+I\+S\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a6625bc4e7ffd535900ef53259cc21651}\label{ssl_8h_a6625bc4e7ffd535900ef53259cc21651}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+timeout@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+timeout}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+timeout@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+timeout}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+timeout()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_handshake\_timeout()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+timeout (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{min,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{max }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set retransmit timeout values for the D\+T\+LS handshake. (D\+T\+LS only, no effect on T\+LS.) 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em min} & Initial timeout value in milliseconds. Default\+: 1000 (1 second). \\
\hline
{\em max} & Maximum timeout value in milliseconds. Default\+: 60000 (60 seconds).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Default values are from R\+FC 6347 section 4.\+2.\+4.\+1.

The \textquotesingle{}min\textquotesingle{} value should typically be slightly above the expected round-\/trip time to your peer, plus whatever time it takes for the peer to process the message. For example, if your R\+TT is about 600ms and you peer needs up to 1s to do the cryptographic operations in the handshake, then you should set \textquotesingle{}min\textquotesingle{} slightly above 1600. Lower values of \textquotesingle{}min\textquotesingle{} might cause spurious resends which waste network resources, while larger value of \textquotesingle{}min\textquotesingle{} will increase overall latency on unreliable network links.

The more unreliable your network connection is, the larger your max / min ratio needs to be in order to achieve reliable handshakes.

Messages are retransmitted up to log2(ceil(max/min)) times. For example, if min = 1s and max = 5s, the retransmit plan goes\+: send ... 1s -\/$>$ resend ... 2s -\/$>$ resend ... 4s -\/$>$ resend ... 5s -\/$>$ give up and return a timeout error. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a193c7bf368780f485e20170c807709e5}\label{ssl_8h_a193c7bf368780f485e20170c807709e5}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+legacy\+\_\+renegotiation@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+legacy\+\_\+renegotiation}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+legacy\+\_\+renegotiation@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+legacy\+\_\+renegotiation}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+legacy\+\_\+renegotiation()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_legacy\_renegotiation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+legacy\+\_\+renegotiation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int}]{allow\+\_\+legacy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Prevent or allow legacy renegotiation. (Default\+: M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+ON) 

M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+ON allows connections to be established even if the peer does not support secure renegotiation, but does not allow renegotiation to take place if not secure. (Interoperable and secure option)

M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+ON allows renegotiations with non-\/upgraded peers. Allowing legacy renegotiation makes the connection vulnerable to specific man in the middle attacks. (See R\+FC 5746) (Most interoperable and least secure option)

M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+R\+E\+A\+K\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+S\+H\+A\+KE breaks off connections if peer does not support secure renegotiation. Results in interoperability issues with non-\/upgraded peers that do not support renegotiation altogether. (Most secure option, interoperability issues)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em allow\+\_\+legacy} & Prevent or allow (S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+ON, S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+ON or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+R\+E\+A\+K\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+S\+H\+A\+KE) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_afc1a81e3fcbea3045b41ce739a47f54e}\label{ssl_8h_afc1a81e3fcbea3045b41ce739a47f54e}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+max\+\_\+version@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+max\+\_\+version}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+max\+\_\+version (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int}]{major,  }\item[{int}]{minor }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the maximum supported version sent from the client side and/or accepted at the server side (Default\+: M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+J\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON, M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON) 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This ignores ciphersuites from higher versions.

With D\+T\+LS, use M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+2 for D\+T\+LS 1.\+0 and M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+3 for D\+T\+LS 1.\+2
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+min\+\_\+version (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int}]{major,  }\item[{int}]{minor }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the minimum accepted S\+S\+L/\+T\+LS protocol version (Default\+: T\+LS 1.\+0) 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Input outside of the S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+X\+X\+X\+X\+X\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON and S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+X\+X\+X\+X\+X\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON range is ignored.

M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+0 (S\+SL v3) should be avoided.

With D\+T\+LS, use M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+2 for D\+T\+LS 1.\+0 and M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+3 for D\+T\+LS 1.\+2
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline

\hline

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a4e54e9ace21beb608bae36ddb81a4fb0}\label{ssl_8h_a4e54e9ace21beb608bae36ddb81a4fb0}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+own\+\_\+cert@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+own\+\_\+cert}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+own\+\_\+cert@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+own\+\_\+cert}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+own\+\_\+cert()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_own\_cert()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+own\+\_\+cert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__x509__crt}{mbedtls\+\_\+x509\+\_\+crt}} $\ast$}]{own\+\_\+cert,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__pk__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+pk\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{pk\+\_\+key }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set own certificate chain and private key. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
own\+\_\+cert should contain in order from the bottom up your certificate chain. The top certificate (self-\/signed) can be omitted.

On server, this function can be called multiple times to provision more than one cert/key pair (eg one E\+C\+D\+SA, one R\+SA with S\+H\+A-\/256, one R\+SA with S\+H\+A-\/1). An adequate certificate will be selected according to the client\textquotesingle{}s advertised capabilities. In case mutliple certificates are adequate, preference is given to the one set by the first call to this function, then second, etc.

On client, only the first call has any effect. That is, only one client certificate can be provisioned. The server\textquotesingle{}s preferences in its Certficate\+Request message will be ignored and our only cert will be sent regardless of whether it matches those preferences -\/ the server can then decide what it wants to do with it.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em own\+\_\+cert} & own public certificate chain \\
\hline
{\em pk\+\_\+key} & own private key\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_psk()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{const unsigned char $\ast$}]{psk,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{psk\+\_\+len,  }\item[{const unsigned char $\ast$}]{psk\+\_\+identity,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{psk\+\_\+identity\+\_\+len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the Pre Shared Key (P\+SK) and the expected identity name. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is mainly useful for clients. Servers will usually want to use {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a1b804626a236e493316c58b048ab5937}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk\+\_\+cb()}}} instead.

Currently clients can only register one pre-\/shared key. In other words, the servers\textquotesingle{} identity hint is ignored. Support for setting multiple P\+S\+Ks on clients and selecting one based on the identity hint is not a planned feature but feedback is welcomed.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em psk} & pointer to the pre-\/shared key \\
\hline
{\em psk\+\_\+len} & pre-\/shared key length \\
\hline
{\em psk\+\_\+identity} & pointer to the pre-\/shared key identity \\
\hline
{\em psk\+\_\+identity\+\_\+len} & identity key length\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a1b804626a236e493316c58b048ab5937}\label{ssl_8h_a1b804626a236e493316c58b048ab5937}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk\+\_\+cb@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk\+\_\+cb}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk\+\_\+cb@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk\+\_\+cb}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk\+\_\+cb()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_psk\_cb()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk\+\_\+cb (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$, const unsigned char $\ast$, size\+\_\+t)}]{f\+\_\+psk,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\+\_\+psk }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the P\+SK callback (server-\/side only). 

If set, the P\+SK callback is called for each handshake where a P\+SK ciphersuite was negotiated. The caller provides the identity received and wants to receive the actual P\+SK data and length.

The callback has the following parameters\+: (void $\ast$parameter, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$ssl, const unsigned char $\ast$psk\+\_\+identity, size\+\_\+t identity\+\_\+len) If a valid P\+SK identity is found, the callback should use {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a50f8bb06a3ec75f6fec4ccc2c1aad151}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+hs\+\_\+psk()}}} on the ssl context to set the correct P\+SK and return 0. Any other return value will result in a denied P\+SK identity.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you set a P\+SK callback using this function, then you don\textquotesingle{}t need to set a P\+SK key and identity using {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a1e185199e3ff613bdd1c8231a19e24fc}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+psk()}}}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+psk} & P\+SK identity function \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+psk} & P\+SK identity parameter \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a0d925033b3a46a48b3f8acc1d743af90}\label{ssl_8h_a0d925033b3a46a48b3f8acc1d743af90}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+read\+\_\+timeout@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+read\+\_\+timeout}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+read\+\_\+timeout()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_read\_timeout()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+read\+\_\+timeout (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{timeout }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the timeout period for \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read()}} (Default\+: no timeout.) 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration context \\
\hline
{\em timeout} & Timeout value in milliseconds. Use 0 for no timeout (default).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
With blocking I/O, this will only work if a non-\/\+N\+U\+LL {\ttfamily f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout} was set with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a8b7442420aef7f1a76fa8c5336362f9e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio()}}}. With non-\/blocking I/O, this will only work if timer callbacks were set with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a335ee78886daf7f8fb369fa925b3cca8}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer\+\_\+cb()}}}.

With non-\/blocking I/O, you may also skip this function altogether and handle timeouts at the application layer. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_aad4f50fc1c0a018fd5eb18fd9621d0d3}\label{ssl_8h_aad4f50fc1c0a018fd5eb18fd9621d0d3}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_renegotiation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int}]{renegotiation }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable / Disable renegotiation support for connection when initiated by peer (Default\+: M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED) 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
It is recommended to always disable renegotation unless you know you need it and you know what you\textquotesingle{}re doing. In the past, there have been several issues associated with renegotiation or a poor understanding of its properties.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Server-\/side, enabling renegotiation also makes the server susceptible to a resource DoS by a malicious client.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em renegotiation} & Enable or disable (M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+ED or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a2d193b15941a556baaf2cb94138d66df}\label{ssl_8h_a2d193b15941a556baaf2cb94138d66df}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+enforced@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+enforced}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+enforced@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+enforced}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+enforced()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_renegotiation\_enforced()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+enforced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int}]{max\+\_\+records }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enforce renegotiation requests. (Default\+: enforced, max\+\_\+records = 16) 

When we request a renegotiation, the peer can comply or ignore the request. This function allows us to decide whether to enforce our renegotiation requests by closing the connection if the peer doesn\textquotesingle{}t comply.

However, records could already be in transit from the peer when the request is emitted. In order to increase reliability, we can accept a number of records before the expected handshake records.

The optimal value is highly dependent on the specific usage scenario.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
With D\+T\+LS and server-\/initiated renegotiation, the Hello\+Request is retransmited every time \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read()}} times out or receives Application Data, until\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item max\+\_\+records records have beens seen, if it is $>$= 0, or
\item the number of retransmits that would happen during an actual handshake has been reached. Please remember the request might be lost a few times if you consider setting max\+\_\+records to a really low value.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
On client, the grace period can only happen during \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read()}}, as opposed to \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a49b7a27a616495d5f0a4fabc3f550dbb}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+renegotiate()}} which always behave as if max\+\_\+record was 0. The reason is, if we receive application data from the server, we need a place to write it, which only happens during \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read()}}.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em max\+\_\+records} & Use M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+E\+G\+O\+T\+I\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+F\+O\+R\+C\+ED if you don\textquotesingle{}t want to enforce renegotiation, or a non-\/negative value to enforce it but allow for a grace period of max\+\_\+records records. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a1785faa0640bd6190c1c17a94b408e31}\label{ssl_8h_a1785faa0640bd6190c1c17a94b408e31}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+period@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+period}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+period@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+period}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+period()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_renegotiation\_period()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+renegotiation\+\_\+period (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{const unsigned char}]{period\mbox{[}8\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set record counter threshold for periodic renegotiation. (Default\+: 2$^\wedge$64 -\/ 256.) 

Renegotiation is automatically triggered when a record counter (outgoing or ingoing) crosses the defined threshold. The default value is meant to prevent the connection from being closed when the counter is about to reached its maximal value (it is not allowed to wrap).

Lower values can be used to enforce policies such as \char`\"{}keys
                must be refreshed every N packets with cipher X\char`\"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em period} & The threshold value\+: a big-\/endian 64-\/bit number. Set to 2$^\wedge$64 -\/ 1 to disable periodic renegotiation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a469cd1c64bbba4be22347bf8874a017e}\label{ssl_8h_a469cd1c64bbba4be22347bf8874a017e}}

\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+cache@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+cache}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+cache@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+cache}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+cache()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_session\_cache()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+cache (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\+\_\+cache,  }\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__session}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$)}]{f\+\_\+get\+\_\+cache,  }\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, const \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__session}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$)}]{f\+\_\+set\+\_\+cache }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the session cache callbacks (server-\/side only) If not set, no session resuming is done (except if session tickets are enabled too). 

The session cache has the responsibility to check for stale entries based on timeout. See R\+FC 5246 for recommendations.

Warning\+: session.\+peer\+\_\+cert is cleared by the S\+S\+L/\+T\+LS layer on connection shutdown, so do not cache the pointer! Either set it to N\+U\+LL or make a full copy of the certificate.

The get callback is called once during the initial handshake to enable session resuming. The get function has the following parameters\+: (void $\ast$parameter, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__session}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$session) If a valid entry is found, it should fill the master of the session object with the cached values and return 0, return 1 otherwise. Optionally peer\+\_\+cert can be set as well if it is properly present in cache entry.

The set callback is called once during the initial handshake to enable session resuming after the entire handshake has been finished. The set function has the following parameters\+: (void $\ast$parameter, const \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__session}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$session). The function should create a cache entry for future retrieval based on the data in the session structure and should keep in mind that the \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__session}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session}} object presented (and all its referenced data) is cleared by the S\+S\+L/\+T\+LS layer when the connection is terminated. It is recommended to add metadata to determine if an entry is still valid in the future. Return 0 if successfully cached, return 1 otherwise.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+cache} & parmater (context) for both callbacks \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+get\+\_\+cache} & session get callback \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+set\+\_\+cache} & session set callback \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a97e547f900979337f4083a8158918fcc}\label{ssl_8h_a97e547f900979337f4083a8158918fcc}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+tickets\+\_\+cb (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a112d1fc2dd4db788592457d14c0c2899}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+ticket\+\_\+write\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{f\+\_\+ticket\+\_\+write,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a48aea353b22e86deece00933ef941536}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+ticket\+\_\+parse\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{f\+\_\+ticket\+\_\+parse,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\+\_\+ticket }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Configure S\+SL session ticket callbacks (server only). (Default\+: none.) 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
On server, session tickets are enabled by providing non-\/\+N\+U\+LL callbacks.

On client, use {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a97e547f900979337f4083a8158918fcc}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+session\+\_\+tickets()}}}.

\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sig\+\_\+hashes@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sig\+\_\+hashes}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sig\+\_\+hashes@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sig\+\_\+hashes}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sig\+\_\+hashes()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_sig\_hashes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sig\+\_\+hashes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{const int $\ast$}]{hashes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the allowed hashes for signatures during the handshake. (Default\+: all available hashes except M\+D5.) 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This only affects which hashes are offered and can be used for signatures during the handshake. Hashes for message authentication and the T\+LS P\+RF are controlled by the ciphersuite, see {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_ac8e4df37cadda8f743ed45501a51fec1}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+ciphersuites()}}}. Hashes used for certificate signature are controlled by the verification profile, see {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a76dc3c312ffd51f6d0ca127b322307bb}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+cert\+\_\+profile()}}}.

This list should be ordered by decreasing preference (preferred hash first).
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em hashes} & Ordered list of allowed signature hashes, terminated by {\ttfamily M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+M\+D\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a38ee2c1e3f232444df5ba3952d7ded33}\label{ssl_8h_a38ee2c1e3f232444df5ba3952d7ded33}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sni@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sni}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sni@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sni}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sni()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_conf\_sni()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+sni (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int($\ast$)(void $\ast$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$, const unsigned char $\ast$, size\+\_\+t)}]{f\+\_\+sni,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\+\_\+sni }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set server side Server\+Name T\+LS extension callback (optional, server-\/side only). 

If set, the Server\+Name callback is called whenever the server receives a Server\+Name T\+LS extension from the client during a handshake. The Server\+Name callback has the following parameters\+: (void $\ast$parameter, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$ssl, const unsigned char $\ast$hostname, size\+\_\+t len). If a suitable certificate is found, the callback must set the certificate(s) and key(s) to use with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa0353666974b1cd19dafb2c2b165d2f2}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+hs\+\_\+own\+\_\+cert()}}} (can be called repeatedly), and may optionally adjust the CA and associated C\+RL with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a33a781dcdc16bd649ea0346a598e9656}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+hs\+\_\+ca\+\_\+chain()}}} as well as the client authentication mode with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a8366b49e25054078b5be139c0ce560d7}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+hs\+\_\+authmode()}}}, then must return 0. If no matching name is found, the callback must either set a default cert, or return non-\/zero to abort the handshake at this point.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em conf} & S\+SL configuration \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+sni} & verification function \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+sni} & verification parameter \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a2eb03afe9b2ca0f144a1c307100dc0ca}\label{ssl_8h_a2eb03afe9b2ca0f144a1c307100dc0ca}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+conf\+\_\+transport (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf,  }\item[{int}]{transport }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the transport type (T\+LS or D\+T\+LS). Default\+: T\+LS. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
For D\+T\+LS, you must either provide a recv callback that doesn\textquotesingle{}t block, or one that handles timeouts, see {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a8b7442420aef7f1a76fa8c5336362f9e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio()}}}. You also need to provide timer callbacks with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a335ee78886daf7f8fb369fa925b3cca8}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer\+\_\+cb()}}}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_get\_max\_frag\_len()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return the maximum fragment length (payload, in bytes). This is the value negotiated with peer if any, or the locally configured value. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
With D\+T\+LS, {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write()}}} will return an error if called with a larger length value. With T\+LS, {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write()}}} will fragment the input if necessary and return the number of bytes written; it is up to the caller to call {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write()}}} again in order to send the remaining bytes if any.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Current maximum fragment length. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+peer\+\_\+cert@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+peer\+\_\+cert}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+peer\+\_\+cert()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_get\_peer\_cert()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__x509__crt}{mbedtls\+\_\+x509\+\_\+crt}}$\ast$ mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+peer\+\_\+cert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return the peer certificate from the current connection. 

Note\+: Can be N\+U\+LL in case no certificate was sent during the handshake. Different calls for the same connection can return the same or different pointers for the same certificate and even a different certificate altogether. The peer cert C\+AN change in a single connection if renegotiation is performed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the current peer certificate 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a935f3ebfb31f988e24a8bf9bcb0fd26b}\label{ssl_8h_a935f3ebfb31f988e24a8bf9bcb0fd26b}}

Return the (maximum) number of bytes added by the record layer\+: header + encryption/\+M\+AC overhead (inc. padding) 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Current maximum record expansion in bytes, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+F\+E\+A\+T\+U\+R\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+V\+A\+I\+L\+A\+B\+LE if compression is enabled, which makes expansion much less predictable 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+session (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__session}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session}} $\ast$}]{session }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Save session in order to resume it later (client-\/side only) Session data is copied to presented session structure. 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Currently, peer certificate is lost in the operation.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_handshake()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Perform the S\+SL handshake. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+AD or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+TE, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+L\+L\+O\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED (see below), or a specific S\+SL error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If this function returns something other than 0 or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D/\+W\+R\+I\+TE, then the ssl context becomes unusable, and you should either free it or call {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a21432367cbce428f10dcb62d9456fa7e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session\+\_\+reset()}}} on it before re-\/using it for a new connection; the current connection must be closed.

If D\+T\+LS is in use, then you may choose to handle M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+H\+E\+L\+L\+O\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+I\+R\+ED specially for logging purposes, as it is an expected return value rather than an actual error, but you still need to reset/free the context. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_aac1583fe56eda081580742999968bbcf}\label{ssl_8h_aac1583fe56eda081580742999968bbcf}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+step@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+step}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+step@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+step}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+step()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_handshake\_step()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake\+\_\+step (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Perform a single step of the S\+SL handshake. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The state of the context (ssl-\/$>$state) will be at the next state after execution of this function. Do not call this function if state is M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+D\+S\+H\+A\+K\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+ER.

If this function returns something other than 0 or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D/\+W\+R\+I\+TE, then the ssl context becomes unusable, and you should either free it or call {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a21432367cbce428f10dcb62d9456fa7e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session\+\_\+reset()}}} on it before re-\/using it for a new connection; the current connection must be closed.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+AD or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+TE, or a specific S\+SL error code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a8560dea66d7830a11874188727ec4c45}\label{ssl_8h_a8560dea66d7830a11874188727ec4c45}}

\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}\label{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl,  }\item[{unsigned char $\ast$}]{buf,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Read at most \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} application data bytes. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context \\
\hline
{\em buf} & buffer that will hold the data \\
\hline
{\em len} & maximum number of bytes to read\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of bytes read, or 0 for E\+OF, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+AD or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+TE, or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+CT (see below), or another negative error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If this function returns something other than a positive value or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D/\+W\+R\+I\+TE or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+CT, then the ssl context becomes unusable, and you should either free it or call {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a21432367cbce428f10dcb62d9456fa7e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session\+\_\+reset()}}} on it before re-\/using it for a new connection; the current connection must be closed.

When this function return M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+CT (which can only happen server-\/side), it means that a client is initiating a new connection using the same source port. You can either treat that as a connection close and wait for the client to resend a Client\+Hello, or directly continue with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake()}}} with the same context (as it has beeen reset internally). Either way, you should make sure this is seen by the application as a new connection\+: application state, if any, should be reset, and most importantly the identity of the client must be checked again. W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG\+: not validating the identity of the client again, or not transmitting the new identity to the application layer, would allow authentication bypass! 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a49b7a27a616495d5f0a4fabc3f550dbb}\label{ssl_8h_a49b7a27a616495d5f0a4fabc3f550dbb}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+renegotiate@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+renegotiate}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+renegotiate@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+renegotiate}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+renegotiate()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_renegotiate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+renegotiate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initiate an S\+SL renegotiation on the running connection. Client\+: perform the renegotiation right now. Server\+: request renegotiation, which will be performed during the next call to \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_aa2c29eeb1deaf5ad9f01a7515006ede5}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+read()}} if honored by client. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, or any \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a4a37e497cd08c896870a42b1b618186e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+handshake()}} return value.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If this function returns something other than 0 or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D/\+W\+R\+I\+TE, then the ssl context becomes unusable, and you should either free it or call {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a21432367cbce428f10dcb62d9456fa7e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session\+\_\+reset()}}} on it before re-\/using it for a new connection; the current connection must be closed. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_set\_bio()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+bio (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{p\+\_\+bio,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a38e2b400d361f42f85833cdc30b3916e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+send\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{f\+\_\+send,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_ac06b19b96b643090c55f19b6c28b10c4}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+recv\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{f\+\_\+recv,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a6d615ca95c8a67d7c5f9d7d256dc09e6}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the underlying B\+IO callbacks for write, read and read-\/with-\/timeout. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+bio} & parameter (context) shared by B\+IO callbacks \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+send} & write callback \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+recv} & read callback \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout} & blocking read callback with timeout.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
One of f\+\_\+recv or f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout can be N\+U\+LL, in which case the other is used. If both are non-\/\+N\+U\+LL, f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout is used and f\+\_\+recv is ignored (as if it were N\+U\+LL).

The two most common use cases are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item non-\/blocking I/O, f\+\_\+recv != N\+U\+LL, f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout == N\+U\+LL
\item blocking I/O, f\+\_\+recv == N\+U\+LL, f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timout != N\+U\+LL
\end{DoxyItemize}

For D\+T\+LS, you need to provide either a non-\/\+N\+U\+LL f\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout callback, or a f\+\_\+recv that doesn\textquotesingle{}t block.

See the documentations of {\ttfamily mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+sent\+\_\+t}, {\ttfamily mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+recv\+\_\+t} and {\ttfamily mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout\+\_\+t} for the conventions those callbacks must follow.

On some platforms, \mbox{\hyperlink{net__sockets_8c_source}{net\+\_\+sockets.\+c}} provides {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{net__sockets_8h_a4841afd0e14f1fd44b82c3a850961ab7}{mbedtls\+\_\+net\+\_\+send()}}}, {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{net__sockets_8h_a03af351ec420bbeb5e91357abcfb3663}{mbedtls\+\_\+net\+\_\+recv()}}} and {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{net__sockets_8h_a67810154d2328a80b146155d8cdecfd9}{mbedtls\+\_\+net\+\_\+recv\+\_\+timeout()}}} that are suitable to be used here. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a15fab95c13a898f32fa69ff2065c1051}\label{ssl_8h_a15fab95c13a898f32fa69ff2065c1051}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+client\+\_\+transport\+\_\+id@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+client\+\_\+transport\+\_\+id}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+client\+\_\+transport\+\_\+id@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+client\+\_\+transport\+\_\+id}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+client\+\_\+transport\+\_\+id()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_set\_client\_transport\_id()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+client\+\_\+transport\+\_\+id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl,  }\item[{const unsigned char $\ast$}]{info,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{ilen }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set client\textquotesingle{}s transport-\/level identification info. (Server only. D\+T\+LS only.) 

This is usually the IP address (and port), but could be anything identify the client depending on the underlying network stack. Used for Hello\+Verify\+Request with D\+T\+LS. This is {\itshape not} used to route the actual packets.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context \\
\hline
{\em info} & Transport-\/level info identifying the client (eg IP + port) \\
\hline
{\em ilen} & Length of info in bytes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
An internal copy is made, so the info buffer can be reused.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+A\+TA if used on client, M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+C\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED if out of memory. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_aa659024cf89e20d6d2248c0626db7ef2}\label{ssl_8h_aa659024cf89e20d6d2248c0626db7ef2}}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em p\+\_\+timer} & parameter (context) shared by timer callbacks \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer} & set timer callback \\
\hline
{\em f\+\_\+get\+\_\+timer} & get timer callback. Must return\+:\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
See the documentation of {\ttfamily mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+set\+\_\+timer\+\_\+t} and {\ttfamily mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+timer\+\_\+t} for the conventions this pair of callbacks must fallow.

On some platforms, \mbox{\hyperlink{timing_8c_source}{timing.\+c}} provides {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{timing_8h_aeb3497ab85adabf7db89d81c34e2ef92}{mbedtls\+\_\+timing\+\_\+set\+\_\+delay()}}} and {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{timing_8h_afb1705e8c4227b0ec03089aa7fc54d9b}{mbedtls\+\_\+timing\+\_\+get\+\_\+delay()}}} that are suitable for using here, except if using an event-\/driven style.

See also the \char`\"{}\+D\+T\+L\+S tutorial\char`\"{} article in our knowledge base. \href{https://tls.mbed.org/kb/how-to/dtls-tutorial}{\tt https\+://tls.\+mbed.\+org/kb/how-\/to/dtls-\/tutorial} 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+setup (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__config}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+config}} $\ast$}]{conf }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set up an S\+SL context for use. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
No copy of the configuration context is made, it can be shared by many \mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} structures.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Modifying the conf structure after it has been used in this function is unsupported!
\end{DoxyWarning}

\hline

\hline

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}\label{ssl_8h_a5bbda87d484de82df730758b475f32e5}} 
\index{ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}!mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write}}
\index{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write@{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write}!ssl.\+h@{ssl.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write()}{mbedtls\_ssl\_write()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmbedtls__ssl__context}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+context}} $\ast$}]{ssl,  }\item[{const unsigned char $\ast$}]{buf,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Try to write exactly \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} application data bytes. 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This function will do partial writes in some cases. If the return value is non-\/negative but less than length, the function must be called again with updated arguments\+: buf + ret, len -\/ ret (if ret is the return value) until it returns a value equal to the last \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} argument.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ssl} & S\+SL context \\
\hline
{\em buf} & buffer holding the data \\
\hline
{\em len} & how many bytes must be written\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of bytes actually written (may be less than len), or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+TE of M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+AD, or another negative error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If this function returns something other than a positive value or M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D/\+W\+R\+I\+TE, the ssl context becomes unusable, and you should either free it or call {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a21432367cbce428f10dcb62d9456fa7e}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+session\+\_\+reset()}}} on it before re-\/using it for a new connection; the current connection must be closed.

When this function returns M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+N\+T\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+T\+E/\+R\+E\+AD, it must be called later with the {\itshape same} arguments, until it returns a positive value.

If the requested length is greater than the maximum fragment length (either the built-\/in limit or the one set or negotiated with the peer), then\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item with T\+LS, less bytes than requested are written.
\item with D\+T\+LS, M\+B\+E\+D\+T\+L\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+S\+L\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+D\+A\+TA is returned. {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ssl_8h_a44fb4dcf45412d667778432836be9150}{mbedtls\+\_\+ssl\+\_\+get\+\_\+max\+\_\+frag\+\_\+len()}}} may be used to query the active maximum fragment length. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
